CREATE TABLE trips (id INT PRIMARY KEY, destination_id INT REFERENCES destinations(id), start_date DATE, end_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (destination_id) REFERENCES destinations(id))

CREATE TABLE bookings (id INT PRIMARY KEY, trip_id INT REFERENCES trips(id), traveler_id INT REFERENCES travelers(id), booking_date DATE, FOREIGN KEY (trip_id) REFERENCES trips(id), FOREIGN KEY (traveler_id) REFERENCES travelers(id))</t><s>UPSERT INTO trips (id, destination_id, start_date, end_date) VALUES (1, 1, '2022-10-01', '2022-10-10') ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE destination_id=1, start_date='2022-10-01', end_date='2022-10-10';</s>

CREATE TABLE airports (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, name STRING, city STRING, country STRING, terminal STRING);

CREATE TABLE destinations (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, name STRING, country STRING, description STRING);

CREATE TABLE airlines (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, name STRING, country STRING, website STRING);</t><s>INSERT INTO destinations (id, name, country, description) VALUES ('b10c2d3c-5018-4fc5-8452-3905f7a57c14', 'Paris', 'France', 'City of Love') ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET name = EXCLUDED.name, country = EXCLUDED.country, description = EXCLUDED.description;</s>

CREATE TABLE airports (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, name STRING, city STRING, country STRING, terminal STRING);</t><s>insert into destinations (id, name, country, description) values ('b10c2d3c-5018-4fc5-8452-3905f7a57c14', 'paris', 'france', 'city of love') on conflict (id) do update set name = excluded.name, country = excluded.country, description = excluded.description;</s>

CREATE TABLE destinations (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, name STRING, country STRING, description STRING);

CREATE TABLE bookings (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, flight_id UUID REFERENCES flights(id), passenger_name STRING, passenger_email STRING, booking_date TIMESTAMP);

CREATE TABLE airlines (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, name STRING, country STRING, website STRING);</t><s>INSERT INTO destinations (id, name, country, description) VALUES ('b10c2d3c-5018-4fc5-8452-3905f7a57c14', 'Paris', 'France', 'City of Love') ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET name = EXCLUDED.name, country = EXCLUDED.country, description = EXCLUDED.description;</s>

CREATE TABLE flights (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, destination_id UUID REFERENCES destinations(id), flight_number STRING, departure_date TIMESTAMP, departure_time TIME, arrival_date TIMESTAMP, arrival_time TIME);

CREATE TABLE destinations (id UUID PRIMARY KEY, name STRING, country STRING, description STRING);</t><s>INSERT INTO bookings (id, flight_id, passenger_name, passenger_email, booking_date) VALUES ('f2c397b6-1c0e-4de1-bd4d-629c06d170cf', 'f687c290-6c32-4ee5-b440-781f7e183a22', 'Alice Smith', 'alice@example.com', '2023-06-10') ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET flight_id = EXCLUDED.flight_id, passenger_name = EXCLUDED.passenger_name, passenger_email = EXCLUDED.passenger_email, booking_date = EXCLUDED.booking_date;</s>
